[2025-12-21T03:02:10Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: OK I know I promised to stop gushing about it. But I have to share this. So I will make a question out of it. On the 6th Nizam Mehboob Ali Khan’s nickname Tees Maar Khan: why did he get that nickname? BTW, to give you more background about the guy. His uncle the prime minister built Falaknuma palace for himself. Mehboob basically asked for an invite to stay at the palace and check it out, and Viqar-ul-Umra agreed. Mehboob starts his visit, days turn into weeks, weeks turn into months, and he doesn’t leave. Eventually Viqar-ul-Umra just offers to “gift” the palace to Mehboob and Mehboob graciously agrees to reimburse _some_ of the cost of construction. With that background, why do you think our man is called Tees Maar Khan?

X was the daughter of Y, who is the subject of this interesting anecdote.
